***черкнуть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:черкнуть.html>черкну́ть</a> (30469)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><span class="maintenance-line" style="color: 777777;">(This etymology is missing or incomplete. Please add to it, or discuss it at the Etymology scriptorium.)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черкнуть.html>черкну́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čerknútʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">черка́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">чёркать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to write, to scribble
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:черкнуть.html>черкну́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:несколько.html>не́сколько</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:слово.html>сло́в</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>čerknútʹ</b> néskolʹko slov</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drop a line</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***чернеть.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чернеть.html>че́рнеть</a> (6476)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čórnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-е́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-étʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернеть.html>черне́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">černétʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:почернеть.html>почерне́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to turn/become/grow black, to blacken</li>
<li>to show black
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:вдали.html>вдали́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чернеть.html>черне́л</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:лес.html>лес</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">vdalí <b>černél</b> les</i> ― <span class="e-translation">the forest showed black in the distance</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">что́-то <b><a href = vnd.unilang:чернеть.html>черне́ло</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдали.html>вдали́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">štó-to <b>černélo</b> vdalí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">something black loomed in the distance; there was a black spot in the distance</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">čórnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернота.html>чернота́</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">černotá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернить.html>черни́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">černítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернявый.html>черня́вый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">černjávyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернеть.html>че́рнеть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čérnetʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернеть.html>че́рнети</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернеть.html>че́рнети</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернеть.html>че́рнетей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">ornithology</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> bluebill, scaup</li></ol>

***черника.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:черника.html>черни́ка</a> (20632)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čórnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ика</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ika</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чернильница.html>черни́льница</a> (11665)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернила.html>черни́ла</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">černíla</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ни́ца</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-níca</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернильница.html>черни́льница</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">černílʹnica</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернильница.html>черни́льницы</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернильница.html>черни́льницы</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернильница.html>черни́льниц</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">inanimate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> inkwell, inkpot <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">container for ink</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">animate<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory<span class="ib-comma">,</span> ethnic slur<span class="ib-comma">,</span> neologism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> white woman who seeks sexual relationships with non-white (usually black or Central Asian) men, mud shark</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чернильный.html>черни́льный</a> (15324)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернила.html>черни́ла</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">černíla</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернильный.html>черни́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">černílʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> ink

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чернильный.html>черни́льный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:карандаш.html>каранда́ш</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>černílʹnyj</b> karandáš</i> ― <span class="e-translation">copying/indelible pencil</span></div></dd>

***чернить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чернить.html>черни́ть</a> (21663)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернить.html>черни́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">černítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зачерни́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">начерни́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">почерни́ть</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">очерни́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to blacken
<dl><dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfectives:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">зачерни́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">začernítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">начерни́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">načernítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">почерни́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">počernítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>to slander, to smear
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чернить.html>черни́ть</a></b> чью́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:репутация.html>репута́цию</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>černítʹ</b> čʹjú-libo reputáciju</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to blacken/soil smb's reputation</span></div></dd>
<dd><span class="nyms perfective"><span class="defdate">Perfective:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">очерни́ть</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">očernítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>

***чернобыль.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чернобыль.html>чернобы́ль</a> (21419)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Equivalent to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">черно-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">černo-</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">black</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*bylь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">herb</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:былинка.html>были́нка</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bylínka</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">blade of grass</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> for the second element.
</p><p>Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ukrainian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Ukrainian language">Ukrainian</a></span> <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="uk">чорно́биль</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="uk-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čornóbylʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Czech_language" class="extiw" title="w:Czech language">Czech</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="cs">černobýl</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернобыль.html>чернобы́ль</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">černobýlʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернобыль.html>чернобы́ля</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернобыль.html>чернобы́ли</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернобыль.html>чернобы́лей</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>wormwood, mugwort <i>(Artemisia vulgaris)</i></li></ol>

***чернобыльский.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чернобыльский.html>черно́быльский</a> (29520)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернобыль.html>черно́быль</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Černóbylʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернобыльский.html>черно́быльский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">černóbylʹskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Chernobyl
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:чернобыльский.html>черно́быльская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:катастрофа.html>катастро́фа</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>černóbylʹskaja</b> katastrófa</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>Chernobyl</b> disaster</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***черновой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:черновой.html>черново́й</a> (23719)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čórnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ово́й</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черновой.html>черново́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">černovój</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">engineering</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rough
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:черновой.html>черново́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:инструмент.html>инструме́нт</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>černovój</b> instrumént</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>roughing</b> tool</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:черновой.html>черново́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:монтаж.html>монта́ж</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>černovój</b> montáž</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>rough</b> cut <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">of a movie</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:черновой.html>черново́е</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:сверло.html>сверло́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>černovóje</b> sverló</i> ― <span class="e-translation">first bit <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in a drill</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>rough</b> bit</span>”)</div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:черновой.html>черново́е</a></b> шлифова́ние</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>černovóje</b> šlifovánije</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>coarse/rough</b> grinding</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> draft
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:черновой.html>черново́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:набросок.html>набро́сок</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>černovój</b> nabrósok</i> ― <span class="e-translation">draft; sketch</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>draft</b> sketch</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***чернокнижник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чернокнижник.html>чернокни́жник</a> (30113)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернокнижник.html>чернокни́жник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">černoknížnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернокнижник.html>чернокни́жника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернокнижник.html>чернокни́жники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернокнижник.html>чернокни́жников</a></b>)
</p>

<li><span class="example-block" style="color:black">― <a href = vnd.unilang:а.html>А</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a>, <span class="example-select" style="background-color: EDF0FF; font-weight: bold;"><a href = vnd.unilang:черномазый.html>чернома́зый</a></span>, ― <a href = vnd.unilang:кричать.html>крича́ла</a> Зина <a href = vnd.unilang:уже.html>уже́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> Ростислава Романовича, ― <a href = vnd.unilang:ты.html>ты</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:самый.html>са́мый</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:гад.html>гад</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:смерть.html>сме́рти</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ненавидеть.html>ненави́жу</a>! </span></li>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">чьрнота</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čĭrnota</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьrnota</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьrnъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">black</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*-ota</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">-ness</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***чернуха.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чернуха.html>черну́ха</a> (30219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čórnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-у́ха</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-úxa</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернуха.html>черну́ха</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">černúxa</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr> or <abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернуха.html>черну́хи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернуха.html>черну́хи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернуха.html>черну́х</a></b>, <i>related adjective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">черну́шный</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> collective</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> the negative aspects of life, e.g. doom, hopelessness, cruelty, poverty, violence</li>
<li>chernukha <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a gloomy genre of Russian horror</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> something painted black, e.g. a postage stamp</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">low  colloquial<span class="ib-comma">,</span> animate</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> dark-complexioned girl with black hair</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> black cumin herb or flower (<i>Nigella sativa</i>), also called <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Roman_coriander" class="extiw" title="w:Roman coriander">Roman coriander</a>, black caraway, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/black_seed" class="extiw" title="w:black seed">black seed</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/nutmeg_flower" class="extiw" title="w:nutmeg flower">nutmeg flower</a> or <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/love_in_the_mist" class="extiw" title="w:love in the mist">love in the mist</a></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> mushroom of <i>Russula adusta</i> species</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">dark-complexioned girl, herb, mushroom</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">черну́шка</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">černúška</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чернь.html>чернь</a> (13709)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черный.html>чёрный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čórnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Doublet of <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">че́рень</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čérenʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернь.html>чернь</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">černʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернь.html>че́рни</a></b>, <i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>mob, populace, riffraff, rabble</li></ol>

***чернящий.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чернящий.html>черня́щий</a> (21663)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чернящий.html>черня́щий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">černjáščij</span>)
</p>

***черпать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:черпать.html>че́рпать</a> (11329)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">чьрпати</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čĭrpati</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьrpati</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*(s)kerp-</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черпать.html>че́рпать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čérpatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">черпну́ть</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to draw; to ladle; to scoop</li></ol>

***черствый.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:черствый.html>чёрствый</a> (15163)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">чьрствъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čĭrstvŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьrstvъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черствый.html>чёрствый</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čórstvyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)черстве́е</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)черстве́й</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>stale</li>
<li>hardhearted, callous <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">emotionally hardened</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бездушный.html>безду́шный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bezdúšnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">нечуткий</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">nečutkij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:черта.html>черта́</a> (554)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">чьрта</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čĭrta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьrta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черта.html>черта́</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čertá</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черта.html>черты́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черта.html>черты́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:черта.html>черт</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>line</li>
<li>boundary, precinct</li>
<li>trait, streak, feature</li>
<li>stroke (particularly of a Chinese character)</li></ol>

***чертеж.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:чертеж.html>чертеж</a> (6230)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">чьртежь</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čĭrtežĭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">mark, verge; plan, drawing</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*čьrtežь</i>. Synchronically analyzable as <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чертить.html>черти́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">čertítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ёж</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-jóž</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru">чертёж</strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">čertjóž</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чертеж.html>чертежа́</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чертеж.html>чертежи́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:чертеж.html>чертеже́й</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>draft, scheme, plan, diagram</li></ol>
